Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Comanche 72/3 (AKA Manche72 revision 3), the final, flown mission release of the Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) Command Module (CM) software for Apollo 13.

The starting point was the source code of Comanche 72 (itself previously reconstructed). Comanche 72 source code was then modified by incorporating changes known from contemporary documentation to have been made between revisions 72 and 72/3. The resulting code assembles to have identical memory-bank checksums as those specified in NASA drawing 2021153G; this gives reasonably high confidence that the changes that have been made are correct. In places where ambiguity exists, this ambiguity is discussed in "## Reconstruction:" comments.

Since no contemporary listings of Comanche 72/3 are available as source material, all comments and labels are approximate. They have been taken from other AGC programs where possible, or, in some places, written from scratch to match what we believe would have been in the original listing.

012727,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
012728,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Manche72 revision 3.
012729,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the final, flown
012730,000006:                                                                                                  ##              release of the software for the Command Module's (CM) Apollo
012731,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 13. No original listings
012732,000008:                                                                                                  ##              of this program are available; instead, this file was recreated
012733,000009:                                                                                                  ##              from a reconstructed copy of Comanche 072. It has been adapted
012734,000010:                                                                                                  ##              such that the resulting bugger words exactly match those
012735,000011:                                                                                                  ##              specified for Manche72 revision 3 in NASA drawing 2021153G,
012736,000012:                                                                                                  ##              which gives relatively high confidence that the reconstruction
012737,000013:                                                                                                  ##              is correct.
012738,000014:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
012739,000015:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
012740,000016:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
012741,000017:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2024-05-19 MAS  Created from Comanche 072.
012742,000018: 
012743,000019:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
012744,000020:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4            DATE - 27 APRIL 1967            ASSEMBLY - PINDISK REV 17
012745,000021:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
012746,000022:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
012747,000023: 
012748,000024:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
012749,000025: 
012750,000026:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
012751,000027:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
012752,000028:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
012753,000029:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
012754,000030: 
012755,000031:                                                                                                  #  THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
012756,000032:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
012757,000033:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
012758,000034:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
012759,000035:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
012760,000036: 
012761,000037:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
012762,000038:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS (THESE
012763,000039:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
012764,000040:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
012765,000041: 
012766,000042:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
012767,000043:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
012768,000044: 
012769,000045:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
012770,000046: 
012771,000047:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
012772,000048:                                                                                                  #  EACH DEPRESSION OF A MAIN (NAVIGATION) KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES
012773,000049:                                                                                                  #  INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO 
012774,000050:                                                                                                  #  CHANNEL 15 (CHANNEL 16).  KEYRUPT1 (KEYRUPT2) PLACES THE KEY
012775,000051:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
012776,000052:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012777,000053: 
012778,000054:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
012779,000055:                                                                                                  #  EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
012780,000056:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
012781,000057:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
012782,000058: 
012783,000059:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
012784,000060:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
012785,000061:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
012786,000062:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
012787,000063:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
012788,000064: 
012789,000065:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
012790,000066: 
012791,000067:                                                                                                  #        IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
012792,000068:                                                                                                  #                1)      ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
012793,000069:                                                                                                  #                2)      EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE
012794,000070:                                                                                                  #                        PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
012795,000071:                                                                                                  #                        RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
012796,000072:                                                                                                  #                        CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
012797,000073:                                                                                                  #                        ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB.  EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
012798,000074:                                                                                                  #                3)      VERB 37.  CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
012799,000075:                                                                                                  #                        SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
012800,000076:                                                                                                  #                        30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
012801,000077:                                                                                                  #                4)      KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
012802,000078:                                                                                                  #                        ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
012803,000079:                                                                                                  #                        THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
012804,000080: 
012805,000081:                                                                                                  #  IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
012806,000082:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
012807,000083:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
012808,000084: 
012809,000085:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
012810,000086: 
012811,000087:                                                                                                  #        EXTERNAL INITIATION:
012812,000088:                                                                                                  #                IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
012813,000089:                                                                                                  #                ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
012814,000090: 
012815,000091:                                                                                                  #        INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
012816,000092:                                                                                                  #                IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
012817,000093:                                                                                                  #                (WITH OCTAL 01501).
012818,000094:                                                                                                  #                IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
012819,000095:                                                                                                  #                CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206).  THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
012820,000096:                                                                                                  #                1)      ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
012821,000097:                                                                                                  #                2)      NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
012822,000098: 
012823,000099:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
012824,000100:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
012825,000101: 
012826,000102:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
012827,000103: 
012828,000104:                                                                                                  #  INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
012829,000105:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
012830,000106:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
012831,000107:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
012832,000108: 
012833,000109:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
012834,000110: 
012835,000111:                                                                                                  #  FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
012836,000112:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.  REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
012837,000113:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
012838,000114:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
012839,000115: 
012840,000116:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR
012841,000117:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
012842,000118: 
012843,000119:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
012844,000120: 
012845,000121:                                                                                                  #  REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
012846,000122:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
012847,000123: 
012848,000124:                                                                                                  #        NVSUB           CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
012849,000125:                                                                                                  #                        OF RELATED INTEREST     NVSBWAIT
012850,000126:                                                                                                  #                                                NVSUBUSY
012851,000127:                                                                                                  #                                                PRENVBSY
012852,000128: 
012853,000129:                                                                                                  #        ENDIDLE         ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
012854,000130:                                                                                                  #                        AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
012855,000131: 
012856,000132:                                                                                                  #        DSPMM           ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
012857,000133:                                                                                                  #                        PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
012858,000134:                                                                                                  #                        (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
012859,000135:                                                                                                  #                        FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
012860,000136: 
012861,000137:                                                                                                  #        BLANKSUB        ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
012862,000138:                                                                                                  #                        COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
012863,000139: 
012864,000140:                                                                                                  #        JAMTERM         ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
012865,000141:                                                                                                  #        JAMPROC         TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V33) FUNCTION.
012866,000142: 
012867,000143:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR         VERBS FOR PERIODIC (1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
012868,000144: 
012869,000145:                                                                                                  #        PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
012870,000146:                                                                                                  #                REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
012871,000147:                                                                                                  #                THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
012872,000148:                                                                                                  #                SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
012873,000149: 
012874,000150:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
012875,000151:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
012876,000152: 
012877,000153:                                                                                                  #        THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
012878,000154:                                                                                                  #        TABLES:.
012879,000155: 
012880,000156:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
012881,000157:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
012882,000158:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
012883,000159: 
012884,000160:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING QUOTATION IS PROVIDED THROUGH THE COURTESY OF THE AUTHORS.
012885,000161: 
012886,000162:                                                                                                  #        ::IT WILL BE PROVED TO THY FACE THAT THOU HAST MEN ABOUT THEE THAT
012887,000163:                                                                                                  #        USUALLY TALK OF A NOUN AND A VERB, AND SUCH ABOMINABLE WORDS AS NO
012888,000164:                                                                                                  #        CHRISTIAN EAR CAN ENDURE TO HEAR.::
012889,000165:                                                                                                  #                                        HENRY 6, ACT 2, SCENE 4
012890,000166: 
012891,000167:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ASSIGNMENTS FOR PINBALL ARE MADE ELSEWHERE
012892,000168: 
012893,000169:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
012894,000170: 
012895,000171:                                                                                                  # DSPCOUNT       ERASE                   DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
012896,000172:                                                                                                  # DECBRNCH       ERASE                   +DEC, -DEC, OCT INDICATOR
012897,000173:                                                                                                  # VERBREG        ERASE                   VERB CODE
012898,000174:                                                                                                  # NOUNREG        ERASE                   NOUN CODE
012899,000175:                                                                                                  # XREG           ERASE                   R1 INPUT BUFFER
012900,000176:                                                                                                  # YREG           ERASE                   R2 INPUT BUFFER
012901,000177:                                                                                                  # ZREG           ERASE                   R3 INPUT BUFFER
012902,000178:                                                                                                  # XREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
012903,000179:                                                                                                  # YREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
012904,000180:                                                                                                  # HITEMOUT       =       YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
012905,000181:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
012906,000182:                                                                                                  # ZREGLP         ERASE                   LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
012907,000183:                                                                                                  # LOTEMOUT       =       ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS,MIN,SEC
012908,000184:                                                                                                  #                                                 MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
012909,000185:                                                                                                  # MODREG         ERASE                   MODE CODE
012910,000186:                                                                                                  # DSPLOCK        ERASE                   KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
012911,000187:                                                                                                  # REQRET         ERASE                   RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
012912,000188:                                                                                                  # LOADSTAT       ERASE                   STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
012913,000189:                                                                                                  # CLPASS         ERASE                   PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
012914,000190:                                                                                                  # NOUT           ERASE                   ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
012915,000191:                                                                                                  # NOUNCADR       ERASE                   MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
012916,000192:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE        ERASE                   N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
012917,000193:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE1       ERASE                   NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR(MATBS) = MONSAVE+1
012918,000194:                                                                                                  # MONSAVE2       ERASE                   NVMONOPT OPTIONS
012919,000195:                                                                                                  # DSPTAB         ERASE   +13D            0-10, DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER. 11-13, C RELAYS
012920,000196:                                                                                                  # CADRSTOR       ERASE                   ENDIDLE STORAGE
012921,000197:                                                                                                  # NVQTEM         ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
012922,000198:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
012923,000199:                                                                                                  # NVBNKTEM       ERASE                   NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
012924,000200:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = NVQTEM+1
012925,000201:                                                                                                  # VERBSAVE       ERASE                   NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
012926,000202:                                                                                                  # DSPLIST        ERASE                   WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
012927,000203:                                                                                                  # EXTVBACT       REASE                   EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
012928,000204:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM1        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
012929,000205:                                                                                                  # DSPTEM2        ERASE   +2              BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
012930,000206: 
012931,000207:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
012932,000208: 
012933,000209:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
012934,000210:                                                                                                  # DSEXIT         =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR DSPIN
012935,000211:                                                                                                  # EXITEM         =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE SELECT
012936,000212:                                                                                                  # BLANKRET       =       INTB15+         RETURN FOR 2BLANK
012937,000213:                                                                                                  # WRDRET         =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR 5BLANK
012938,000214:                                                                                                  # WDRET          =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR DSPWD
012939,000215:                                                                                                  # DECRET         =       INTBIT15        RETURN FOR PUTCOM(DEC LOAD)
012940,000216:                                                                                                  # 21/22REG       =       INTBIT15        TEMP FOR CHARIN
012941,000217:                                                                                                  # UPDATRET       =       POLISH          RETURN FOR UPDATNN, UPDATVB
012942,000218:                                                                                                  # CHAR           =       POLISH          TEMP FOR CHARIN
012943,000219:                                                                                                  # ERCNT          =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET
012944,000220:                                                                                                  # DECOUNT        =       POLISH          COUNTER FOR SCALING AND DISPLAY (DEC)
012945,000221:                                                                                                  # SGNON          =       VBUF            TEMP FOR +,- ON
012946,000222:                                                                                                  # NOUNTEM        =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR MIXNOUN FETCH
012947,000223:                                                                                                  # DISTEM         =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR OCTAL DISPLAY VERBS
012948,000224:                                                                                                  # DECTEM         =       VBUF            COUNTER FOR FETCH (DEC DISPLAY VERBS)
012949,000225:                                                                                                  # SGNOFF         =       VBUF +1         TEMP FOR +,- ON
012950,000226:                                                                                                  # NVTEMP         =       VBUF +1         TEMP FOR NVSUB
012951,000227:                                                                                                  # SFTEMP1        =       VBUF +1         STORAGE FOR SF CONST HI PART (=SFTEMP2-1)
012952,000228:                                                                                                  # HITEMIN        =       VBUF +1         TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS,MIN,SEC
012953,000229:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = LOTEMIN-1.
012954,000230:                                                                                                  # CODE           =       VBUF +2         FOR DSPIN
012955,000231:                                                                                                  # SFTEMP2        =       VBUF +2         STORAGE FOR SF CONST LO PART (=SFTEMP1+1)
012956,000232:                                                                                                  # LOTEMIN        =       VBUF +2         TEMP FOR LOAD OF HRS,MIN,SEC
012957,000233:                                                                                                  #                                                MUST = HITEMIN+1.
012958,000234:                                                                                                  # MIXTEMP        =       VBUF +3         FOR MIXNOUN DATA
012959,000235:                                                                                                  # SIGNRET        =       VBUF +3         RETURN FOR +,- ON
012960,000236:                                                                                                  #  ALSO MIXTEMP+1 = VBUF+4, MIXTEMP+2 = VBUF+5.
012961,000237:                                                                                                  # ENTRET         =       DOTINC          EXIT FROM ENTER
012962,000238:                                                                                                  # WDCNT          =       DOTRET          CHAR COUNTER FOR DSPWD
012963,000239:                                                                                                  # INREL          =       DOTRET          INPUT BUFFER SELECTOR (X,Y,Z, REG )
012964,000240:                                                                                                  # DSPMMTEM       =       MATINC          DSPCOUNT SAVE FOR DSPMM
012965,000241:                                                                                                  # MIXBR          =       MATINC          INDICATOR FOR MIXED OR NORMAL NOUN
012966,000242:                                                                                                  # TEM1           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
012967,000243:                                                                                                  # DSREL          =       TEM1            REL ADDRESS FOR DSPIN
012968,000244:                                                                                                  # TEM2           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
012969,000245:                                                                                                  # DSMAG          =       TEM2            MAGNITUDE STORE FOR DSPIN
012970,000246:                                                                                                  # IDADDTEM       =       TEM2            MIXNOUN INDIRECT ADDRESS STORAGE
012971,000247:                                                                                                  # TEM3           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
012972,000248:                                                                                                  # COUNT          =       TEM3            FOR DSPIN
012973,000249:                                                                                                  # TEM4           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
012974,000250:                                                                                                  # LSTPTR         =       TEM4            LIST POINTER FOR GRABUSY
012975,000251:                                                                                                  # RELRET         =       TEM4            RETURN FOR RELDSP
012976,000252:                                                                                                  # FREERET        =       TEM4            RETURN FOR FREEDSP
012977,000253:                                                                                                  # DSPWDRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR DSPSIGN
012978,000254:                                                                                                  # SEPSCRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPSEC
012979,000255:                                                                                                  # SEPMNRET       =       TEM4            RETURN FOR SEPMIN
012980,000256:                                                                                                  # TEM5           ERASE                   EXEC TEMP
012981,000257:                                                                                                  # NOUNADD        =       TEM5            TEMP STORAGE FOR NOUN ADDRESS
012982,000258:                                                                                                  # NNADTEM        ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN ADDRESS TABLE ENTRY
012983,000259:                                                                                                  # NNTYPTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR NOUN TYPE TABLE ENTRY
012984,000260:                                                                                                  # IDAD1TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
012985,000261:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD2TEM-1, = IDAD3TEM-2.
012986,000262:                                                                                                  # IDAD2TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
012987,000263:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+1, = IDAD3TEM-1.
012988,000264:                                                                                                  # IDAD3TEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR INDIR ADRESS TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN)
012989,000265:                                                                                                  #                                        MUST = IDAD1TEM+2, = IDAD2TEM+1.
012990,000266:                                                                                                  # RUTMXTEM       ERASE                   TEMP FOR SF ROUT TABLE ENTRY (MIXNN ONLY)
012991,000267: 
012992,000268:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
012993,000269:

012995,000271: 
012996,000272:                                                                                                  #        MPAC, THRU MPAC +6
012997,000273:                                                                                                  #        BUF, +1, +2
012998,000274:                                                                                                  #        BUF2, +1, +2
012999,000275:                                                                                                  #        MPTEMP
013000,000276:                                                                                                  #        ADDRWD
013001,000277:

013003,000279: 
013004,000280:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013005,000281: 
013006,000282:                                                                                                  # DSPCNT         ERASE                   COUNTER FOR DSPOUT
013007,000283:                                                                                                  # UPLOCK         ERASE                   BIT1 = UPLINK INTERLOCK (ACTIVATED BY
013008,000284:                                                                                                  #                                        RECEPTION OF A BAD MESSAGE IN UPLINK)
013009,000285: 
013010,000286:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013011,000287: 
013012,000288:                                                                                                  #  TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013013,000289: 
013014,000290:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP1       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013015,000291:                                                                                                  # DSRUPTEM       =       WAITEXIT        TEMP FOR DSPOUT
013016,000292:                                                                                                  # KEYTEMP2       =       RUPTAGN         TEMP FOR KEYRUPT, UPRUPT
013017,000293: 
013018,000294:                                                                                                  #  END OF TEMPORARIES FOR PINBALL INTERRUPT ACTION
013019,000295: 
013020,000296:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
013021,000297:                                                                                                  #        0               10000
013022,000298:                                                                                                  #        1               00001
013023,000299:                                                                                                  #        9               01001
013024,000300:                                                                                                  #        VERB            10001
013025,000301:                                                                                                  #        ERROR RES       10010
013026,000302:                                                                                                  #        KEY RLSE        11001
013027,000303:                                                                                                  #        +               11010
013028,000304:                                                                                                  #        -               11011
013029,000305:                                                                                                  #        ENTER           11100
013030,000306:                                                                                                  #        CLEAR           11110
013031,000307:                                                                                                  #        NOUN            11111
013032,000308: 
013033,000309:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL.  SET OUT0 TO AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
013034,000310:                                                                                                  #  A-S   SELECT A RELAYWORD.  THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
013035,000311:                                                                                                  #        ENERGIZED.
013036,000312:                                                                                                  #  B     FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
013037,000313:                                                                                                  #  C-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
013038,000314:                                                                                                  #  D-S   5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
013039,000315: 
013040,000316:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
013041,000317:                                                                                                  #        MD1             MD2 (MAJOR MODE)
013042,000318:                                                                                                  #        VD1             VD2 (VERB)                      ND1             ND2 (NOUN)
013043,000319:                                                                                                  #        R1D1            R1D2            R1D3            R1D4            R1D5 (R1)
013044,000320:                                                                                                  #        R2D1            R2D2            R2D3            R2D4            R2D5 (R2)
013045,000321:                                                                                                  #        R3D1            R3D2            R3D3            R3D4            R3D5 (R3)
013046,000322: 
013047,000323:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
013048,000324: 
013049,000325:                                                                                                  #        MD1     25              R2D1    11              ALL ARE OCTAL
013050,000326:                                                                                                  #        MD2     24              R2D2    10
013051,000327:                                                                                                  #        VD1     23              R2D3    7
013052,000328:                                                                                                  #        VD2     22              R2D4    6
013053,000329:                                                                                                  #        ND1     21              R2D5    5
013054,000330:                                                                                                  #        ND2     20              R3D1    4
013055,000331:                                                                                                  #        R1D1    16              R3D2    3
013056,000332:                                                                                                  #        R1D2    15              R3D3    2
013057,000333:                                                                                                  #        R1D3    14              R3D4    1
013058,000334:                                                                                                  #        R1D4    13              R3D5    0
013059,000335:                                                                                                  #        R1D5    12
013060,000336: 
013061,000337:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
013062,000338: 
013063,000339:                                                                                                  #        DSPTAB          RELAYWD         BIT11           BITS 10-6       BITS 5-1
013064,000340:                                                                                                  #        RELADD
013065,000341:                                                                                                  #        10              1011                            MD1 (25)        MD2  (24)
013066,000342:                                                                                                  #        9               1010                            VD1 (23)        VD2  (22)
013067,000343:                                                                                                  #        8               1001                            ND1 (21)        ND2  (20)
013068,000344:                                                                                                  #        7               1000                                            R1D1 (16)
013069,000345:                                                                                                  #        6               0111            +R1             R1D2 (15)       R1D3 (14)
013070,000346:                                                                                                  #        5               0110            -R1             R1D4 (13)       R1D5 (12)
013071,000347:                                                                                                  #        4               0101            +R2             R2D1 (11)       R2D2 (10)
013072,000348:                                                                                                  #        3               0100            -R2             R2D3 (7)        R2D4 (6)
013073,000349:                                                                                                  #        2               0011                            R2D5 (5)        R3D1 (4)
013074,000350:                                                                                                  #        1               0010            +R3             R3D2 (3)        R3D3 (2)
013075,000351:                                                                                                  #        0               0001            -R3             R3D4 (1)        R3D5 (0)
013076,000352:                                                                                                  #                        0000        NO RELAYWORD
013077,000353: 
013078,000354:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
013079,000355: 
013080,000356:                                                                                                  #        BLANK   00000
013081,000357:                                                                                                  #        0       10101
013082,000358:                                                                                                  #        1       00011
013083,000359:                                                                                                  #        2       11001
013084,000360:                                                                                                  #        3       11011
013085,000361:                                                                                                  #        4       01111
013086,000362:                                                                                                  #        5       11110
013087,000363:                                                                                                  #        6       11100
013088,000364:                                                                                                  #        7       10011
013089,000365:                                                                                                  #        8       11101
013090,000366:                                                                                                  #        9       11111
013091,000367: 
013092,000368:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
013093,000369: 
013094,000370:                                                                                                  #        KEY RELEASE LIGHT       -       BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
013095,000371:                                                                                                  #        VERB/NOUN FLASH         -       BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
013096,000372:                                                                                                  #        OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT    -       BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
013097,000373: 
013098,000374:                                                                                                  #  START OF EXECUTIVE SECTION OF PINBALL
013099,000375: 
013100,000376: 40,2000                                           BANK     40                                    
013101,000377: 40,2000                                           SETLOC   PINBALL1                              
013102,000378: 40,2000                                           BANK                                           
013103,000379: 
013104,000380: 40,2000                                           COUNT    40/PIN                                
013105,000381: 
013106,000382: 40,2000           35033        CHARIN             CAF      ONE                                   #  BLOCK DISPLAY SYST
013107,000383: 40,2001           57012                           XCH      DSPLOCK                               #  MAKE DSP SYST BUSY, BUT SAVE OLD
013108,000384: 40,2002           54115                           TS       21/22REG                              #  C(DSPLOCK) FOR ERROR LIGHT RESET.
013109,000385: 40,2003           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ALL KEYS EXCEPT ER TURN ON KR LITE IF
013110,000386: 40,2004           02006                           TC       +2                                    #  CADRSTOR IS FULL.  THIS REMINDS OPERATOR
013111,000387: 40,2005           02013                           TC       CHARIN2                               #  TO RE-ESTABLISH A FLASHING DISPLAY
013112,000388: 40,2006           42057                           CS       ELRCODE1                              #  WHICH HE HAS OBSCURED WITH DISPLAYS OF
013113,000389: 40,2007           60154                           AD       MPAC                                  #  HIS OWN (SEE REMARKS PRECEDING ROUTINE
013114,000390: 40,2010           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  VBRELDSP).
013115,000391: 40,2011           12013                           BZF      CHARIN2                               
013116,000392: 40,2012           04410                           TC       RELDSPON                              
013117,000393: 40,2013           56154        CHARIN2            XCH      MPAC                                  
013118,000394: 40,2014           54117                           TS       CHAR                                  
013119,000395: 40,2015           50000                           INDEX    A                                     
013120,000396: 40,2016           02017                           TC       +1                                    #    INPUT CODE      FUNCTION
013121,000397: 40,2017           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        0
013122,000398: 40,2020           02076                           TC       NUM                                   #        1
013123,000399: 40,2021           02076                           TC       NUM                                   #        2
013124,000400: 40,2022           02076                           TC       NUM                                   #        3
013125,000401: 40,2023           02076                           TC       NUM                                   #        4

013128,000404: 40,2026           02076                           TC       NUM                                   #        7

013132,000408: 40,2032           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        13
013133,000409: 40,2033           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        14
013134,000410: 40,2034           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        15
013135,000411: 40,2035           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        16
013136,000412: 40,2036           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        17
013137,000413: 40,2037           02074                           TC       NUM        -2                         #        20              0

013143,000419: 40,2045           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        26
013144,000420: 40,2046           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #        27

013153,000429: 
013154,000430: 40,2057           00022        ELRCODE1           OCT      22                                    
013155,000431: 40,2060           04715        ENTERJMP           TC       POSTJUMP                              
013156,000432: 40,2061           62002                           CADR     ENTER                                 
013157,000433: 
013158,000434: 40,2062           10777        89TEST             CCS      DSPCOUNT                              
013159,000435: 40,2063           02067                           TC       +4                                    #  +
013160,000436: 40,2064           02067                           TC       +3                                    #  +0
013161,000437: 40,2065           05233                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #  - BLOCK DATA IN IF DSPCOUNT IS - OR -0
013162,000438: 40,2066           05233                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #  -0
013163,000439: 40,2067           36214                           CAF      THREE                                 
013164,000440: 40,2070           71000                           MASK     DECBRNCH                              
013165,000441: 40,2071           10000                           CCS      A                                     
013166,000442: 40,2072           02076                           TC       NUM                                   #  IF DECBRNCH IS +, 8 OR 9 OK
013167,000443: 40,2073           03341                           TC       CHARALRM                              #  IF DECBRNCH IS +0, REJECT 8 OR 9
013168,000444: 
013169,000445:                                                                                                  #  NUM ASSEMBLES OCTAL 3 BITS AT A TIME.  FOR DECIMAL IT CONVERTS INCOMING
013170,000446:                                                                                                  #  WORD AS A FRACTION, KEEPING RESULTS TO DP.
013171,000447:                                                                                                  #  OCTAL RESULTS ARE LEFT IN XREG, YREG, OR ZREG.  HI PART OF DEC IN XREG,
013172,000448:                                                                                                  #  YREG, ZREG.  THE LOW PARTS IN XREGLP, YREGLP, OR ZREGLP)
013173,000449:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH IS LEFT AT +0 FOR OCT, +1 FOR + DEC, +2 FOR - DEC.
013174,000450:                                                                                                  #  IF DSPCOUNT WAS LEFT -, NO MORE DATA IS ACCEPTED.
013175,000451: 
013176,000452: 40,2074           35035                           CAF      ZERO

013182,000458: 40,2102           05233                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #  -0
013183,000459: 40,2103           02225                           TC       GETINREL                              
013184,000460: 40,2104           11015                           CCS      CLPASS                                #  IF CLPASS IS + OR +0, MAKE IT +0.
013185,000461: 40,2105           35035                           CAF      ZERO

013768,001044: 
013769,001045: 41,2351           04715        GODSPALM           TC       POSTJUMP                              
013770,001046: 41,2352           61325                           CADR     DSPALARM                              
013771,001047: 
013772,001048:                                                                                                  #  NOUN TABLES
013773,001049: 
013774,001050:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
013775,001051:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE ECADR FOR EACH NOUN.
013776,001052:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.  - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR (E OR F) TO
013777,001053:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED.  -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED.  -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
013778,001054:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
013779,001055: 
013780,001056:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS (IDADDREL) IN LOW
013781,001057:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
013782,001058: 
013783,001059:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
013784,001060: 
013785,001061:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE,  M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
013786,001062:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
013787,001063:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
013788,001064: 
013789,001065:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,           M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER    3 COMPONENT CASE
013790,001066:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
013791,001067:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
013792,001068:                                                                                                  #                        N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER    2 COMPONENT CASE
013793,001069:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
013794,001070:                                                                                                  #                        P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER    1 COMPONENT CASE
013795,001071: 
013796,001072:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE (IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
013797,001073:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.  IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
013798,001074:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
013799,001075: 
013800,001076:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
013801,001077:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
013802,001078: 
013803,001079:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE (RUTMXTAB) FOR MIXED
013804,001080:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY.  THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN.  THE FORM IS,
013805,001081: 
013806,001082:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
013807,001083: 
013808,001084:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER          3 COMPONENT CASE
013809,001085:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
013810,001086:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
013811,001087:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER          2 COMPONENT CASE
013812,001088:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
013813,001089: 
013814,001090:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
013815,001091:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
013816,001092:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
013817,001093: 
013818,001094:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
013819,001095:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED.  ALARM IF VIOLATION.
013820,001096: 
013821,001097:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
013822,001098:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER.  IF NOT, ALARM.
013823,001099: 
013824,001100:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAY VERBS
013825,001101: 
013826,001102: 41,2353           45032        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
013827,001103: 41,2354           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
013828,001104: 41,2355           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
013829,001105: 41,2356           40002                           CS       2

014015,001291:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING IS ATYPICAL SF ROUTINE.  IT USES MPAC.  LEAVES RESU

014022,001298:                                                                                                  #  DEGOUTSF SCALES BY .18 THE LOW 14 BITS OF ANGLE, ADDING .18 FOR
014023,001299:                                                                                                  #  NUMBERS IN THE NEGATIVE (AGC) RANGE.

014030,001306: 40,2523           02566                           TC       DEGCOM                                
014031,001307: 
014032,001308:                                                                                                  #  OPDEGOUT SCALES BY .45 (THE RANGE IS 90 DEGREES) AND ADDS A 20 DEG BIAS.

014035,001311: 40,2525           56154                           XCH      MPAC                                  #  IF POS OR POS 0 THEN ADD BIAS AND

014124,001400:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ROUTINE DISPLAYS TWO CONTIGUOUS SP POSITIVE INTEGERS
014125,001401:                                                                                                  #  AS TWO POSITIVE DECIMAL INTEGERS IN RXD1-RXD2 AND RXD4-RXD5 (RXD3 IS
014126,001402:                                                                                                  #  BLANKED).  THE INTEGER IN THE LOWER NUMBERED ADDRESS IS DISPLAYED IN

014953,002229: 42,3517           55041                           TS       VERBSAVE                              #   IN CASE OPERATOR EXECUTED A LOWER LOAD
014954,002230: 42,3520           04161                           TC       ALMCYCLE                              #   VERB.  ALARM AND RECYCLE.
014955,002231: 42,3521                        ENDHMSS            EQUALS                                         
014956,002232: 
014957,002233:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY.  IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
014958,002234:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
014959,002235:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
014960,002236:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
014961,002237:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
014962,002238: 
014963,002239:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
014964,002240:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET.  IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
014965,002241:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE.  IT SAVES
014966,002242:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED.  BIT 15 OF
014967,002243:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT).  BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
014968,002244:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
014969,002245:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT).  IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
014970,002246: 
014971,002247:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON (+=ON, +0=OFF)
014972,002248:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
014973,002249:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
014974,002250: 
014975,002251:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
014976,002252:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
014977,002253: 
014978,002254:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
014979,002255:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
014980,002256: 
014981,002257:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW
014982,002258:

015523,002799: 40,3360           63372                           AD       VBSP2LD*                              #  DEC 22
