015535,002811: 
015536,002812:                                                                                                  #  VBRESEQ WAKES ENDIDLE AT SAME LINE AS FINAL ENTER OF LOAD (L+3).
015537,002813:                                                                                                  #  (MAIN USE IS INTENDED AS RESPONSE TO INTERNALLY INITIATED FLASHING
015538,002814:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAYS IN ENDIDLE.  SHOULD NOT BE USED WITH LOAD VERBS, PLEASE PERFORM,
015539,002815:                                                                                                  #  OR PLEASE MARK VERBS BECAUSE THEY ALREADY USE L+3 IN ANOTHER CONTEXT.)
015540,002816: 
015541,002817: 40,3373           45035        VBRESEQ            CS       ZERO                                  #  MAKE IT LOOK LIKE DATA IN.
015542,002818: 40,3374           03350                           TC       VBPROC     +1                         
015543,002819: 
015544,002820:                                                                                                  #  FLASH IS TURNED OFF BY PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE,
015545,002821:                                                                                                  #  END OF LOAD.
015546,002822: 
015547,002823:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
015548,002824: 
015549,002825:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
015550,002826: 
015551,002827:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
015552,002828:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
015553,002829:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
015554,002830:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
015555,002831: 
015556,002832:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
015557,002833:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
015558,002834:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
015559,002835: 
015560,002836:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
015561,002837:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
015562,002838:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
015563,002839:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
015564,002840:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
015565,002841:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
015566,002842:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES.  HITTING KEYRLSE WILL
015567,002843:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
015568,002844:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
015569,002845:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
015570,002846:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
015571,002847: 
015572,002848: 40,3375           45031        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
015573,002849: 40,3376           00006                           EXTEND                                         
015574,002850: 40,3377           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
015575,002851: 40,3400           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
015576,002852: 40,3401           35016                           CAF      BIT14                                 
015577,002853: 40,3402           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
015578,002854: 40,3403           10000                           CCS      A                                     
015579,002855: 40,3404           03413                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
015580,002856: 40,3405           04473        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
015581,002857: 40,3406           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
015582,002858: 40,3407           03411                           TC       +2                                    #        DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
015583,002859: 40,3410           05233                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015584,002860: 40,3411           04715                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
015585,002861: 40,3412           21272                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
015586,002862: 40,3413           35035        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
015587,002863: 40,3414           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #        JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
015588,002864: 40,3415           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #        TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
015589,002865: 40,3416           05233                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #        CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
015590,002866: 40,3417           04516                           TC       RELDSP1                               
015591,002867: 40,3420           05233                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015592,002868: 
015593,002869: 40,3421                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
015594,002870: 
015595,002871:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUBROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER.  IT CAN BE
015596,002872:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
015597,002873:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
015598,002874:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
015599,002875:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
015600,002876: 
015601,002877:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
015602,002878:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
015603,002879:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
015604,002880: 
015605,002881:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
015606,002882:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
015607,002883: 
015608,002884:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015609,002885:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE.  THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
015610,002886:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
015611,002887:                                                                                                  #  ACTION).  IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY (RETURN WITH NO
015612,002888:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
015613,002889: 
015614,002890:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
015615,002891:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
015616,002892:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
015617,002893:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
015618,002894: 
015619,002895:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
015620,002896:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
015621,002897:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
015622,002898:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
015623,002899:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
015624,002900:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
015625,002901:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
015626,002902: 
015627,002903:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
015628,002904:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
015629,002905: 
015630,002906:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
015631,002907:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
015632,002908: 
015633,002909:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
015634,002910:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
015635,002911: 
015636,002912:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
015637,002913:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK).  FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
015638,002914:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THEREGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
015639,002915:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
015640,002916:                                                                                                  #  NOUN.  GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
015641,002917:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS.  THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
015642,002918:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
015643,002919: 
015644,002920:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL
015645,002921:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L.  IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
015646,002922:                                                                                                  #  A.  AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
015647,002923:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
015648,002924:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L.  IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
015649,002925:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS.  (THIS VERB
015650,002926:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.)  IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
015651,002927:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
015652,002928:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB.  IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
015653,002929:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
015654,002930: 
015655,002931:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
015656,002932:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET.  (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
015657,002933: 
015658,002934:    4170                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
015659,002935: 
015660,002936:    4170                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
015661,002937: 
015662,002938:    4170           22007        NVSUB              LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
015663,002939:    4171           54123        NVMONOPT           TS       NVTEMP

015690,002966:    4217           05243                           TC       SUPDXCHZ                              #  DTCB WITH SUPERBIT SWITCHING
015691,002967:

015697,002973:                                                                                                  #  -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY

015736,003012:                                                                                                  #                 USES MPAC, +1, +2).

015742,003018: 41,3574           55013                           TS       REQRET                                #  BE EXECUTED BY OPERATOR.

015753,003029: 41,3607           30157                           CA       MPAC       +3                         #  BOTH AND GO TO ENTPAS0.

015763,003039:                                                                                                  #  IF INTERNAL MACH CADR TO BE SPECIFIED, MPAC+2 WILL BE PLACED INTO
015764,003040:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN ENTPAS0 (INTMCTBS).
015765,003041: 
015766,003042:    4220                                           SETLOC   NVSUBEND   +2                         
015767,003043:    4220                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
015768,003044:                                                                                                  #  FORCE BIT 15 OF MONSAVE1 TO 1.
015769,003045:    4220           35015        KILMONON           CAF      BIT15                                 #        THIS IS THE KILL MONITOR BIT.
015770,003046:    4221           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
015771,003047:                                                                                                  #        MONITOR BIT.
015772,003048:    4222           00002                           TC       Q                                     
015773,003049: 
015774,003050:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT      +0      INACTIVE (WAITING FOR DATA).  SET BY NVSUB
015775,003051:                                                                                                  #                +1      PROCEED NO DATA.  SET BY SPECIAL VERB
015776,003052:                                                                                                  #                -1      TERMINATE       SET BY SPECIAL VERB
015777,003053:                                                                                                  #                -0      DATA IN         SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
015778,003054:                                                                                                  #                        OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
015779,003055: 
015780,003056:                                                                                                  #  L TC ENDIDLE (FIXED FIXED)
015781,003057:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
015782,003058:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED.  ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
015783,003059:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
015784,003060:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOB SLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
015785,003061:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
015786,003062:                                                                                                  #        L+1     FOR TERMINATE
015787,003063:                                                                                                  #        L+2     FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
015788,003064:                                                                                                  #        L+3     FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
015789,003065:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
015790,003066: 
015791,003067:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP
015792,003068:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
015793,003069:                                                                                                  #        1)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
015794,003070:                                                                                                  #                EXCEEDED.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
015795,003071:                                                                                                  #        2)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
015796,003072:                                                                                                  #                NVSUBUSY.
015797,003073: 
015798,003074:    4223           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
015799,003075:    4224           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
015800,003076:    4225           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
015801,003077:    4226           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
015802,003078:    4227           75070                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
015803,003079:    4230           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
015804,003080:    4231           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
015805,003081:    4232           05211                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
015806,003082: 
015807,003083:    4233           05233        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
015808,003084: 
015809,003085:    4234           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
015810,003086:    4235           04243                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.
015811,003087:    4236           00002                           TC       Q                                     
015812,003088:    4237           04243                           TC       DSPABORT                              
015813,003089: 
015814,003090:    4240           11043        ISLIST+0           CCS      DSPLIST                               #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
015815,003091:    4241           04243                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF DSPLIST = +0.
015816,003092:    4242           00002                           TC       Q                                     
015817,003093:    4243           05725        DSPABORT           TC       POODOO                                
015818,003094:    4244           21206                           OCT      21206                                 #  SECOND JOB TRYING TO GO TO SLEEP
015819,003095:

015850,003126:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB BLANKS ANY COMBINATION OF R1, R2, R3.
015851,003127:                                                                                                  #  CALL WITH BLANKING CODE IN A.
015852,003128:                                                                                                  #  BIT1=1 BLANKS R1, BIT2=1 BLANKS R2, BIT3=1 BLANKS R3.

015957,003233:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED), TERMINATE VERB IS EXECUTED, OR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA VERB IS
015958,003234:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED.  IT WAKES UP JOB THAT DID TC ENDIDLE.

015961,003237:                                                                                                  #  LIGHT IF DSPLIST IS EMPTY (LEAVES KEY RLSE LIGHT ALONE IF NOT EMPTY).

016102,003378: 
016103,003379:                                                                                                  #  IF MPAC, +1 ARE EACH +NZ OR +0 AND C(A)=-0, SHORTMP WRONGLY GIVES +0.
016104,003380:                                                                                                  #  IF MPAC, +1 ARE EACH -NZ OR -0 AND C(A)=+0, SHORTMP WRONGLY GIVES +0.

016106,003382:                                                                                                  #  SETTING RESULT TO -0.
016107,003383:

016109,003385:                                                                                                  #  WHEN THEY CONTAIN THE SF CONSTANTS.)
016110,003386: 
016111,003387:    4431           54135        PRSHRTMP           TS       MPTEMP

016113,003389:    4433           30135                           CA       MPTEMP                                #  C(A) +,  DO REGULAR SHORTMP
016114,003390:    4434           17257                           TCF      SHORTMP    +1                         #  C(A) +0, DO REGULAR SHORTMP

016123,003399:    4444           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016124,003400:    4445           05011                           WOR      DSALMOUT

016126,003402:

016128,003404:    4450           00006                           EXTEND                                         
016129,003405:    4451           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
016130,003406:    4452           00002                           TC       Q                                     
016131,003407: 
016132,003408:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
016133,003409: 
016134,003410:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
016135,003411:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR.  THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
016136,003412:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
016137,003413:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
016138,003414: 
016139,003415:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016140,003416:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.      1)      BY ENDIDLE
016141,003417:                                                                                                  #                2)      BY NVSUBUSY
016142,003418:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
016143,003419:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME.  IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016144,003420:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY AJOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
016145,003421:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
016146,003422: 
016147,003423:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
016148,003424:                                                                                                  #                        CAF             V/N
016149,003425:                                                                                                  #        L               TC              NVSUB
016150,003426:                                                                                                  #        L+1             RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
016151,003427:                                                                                                  #        L+2             RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
016152,003428: 
016153,003429:                                                                                                  #  A ROUTINE CALLED NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL) TO PUT
016154,003430:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
016155,003431:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM.  NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
016156,003432:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
016157,003433:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
016158,003434: 
016159,003435:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
016160,003436:                                                                                                  #        CAF     WAKEFCADR
016161,003437:                                                                                                  #        TC      NVSUBUSY
016162,003438:                                                                                                  #  .
016163,003439: 
016164,003440:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
016165,003441:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION).  IT IS
016166,003442:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
016167,003443:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
016168,003444: 
016169,003445:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
016170,003446:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL.  IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
016171,003447:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
016172,003448: 
016173,003449:                                                                                                  #        1)      DSPLIST NOT= +0.  THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
016174,003450:                                                                                                  #                IS EXCEEDED.
016175,003451:                                                                                                  #        2)      CADRSTOR NOT= +0.  THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING
016176,003452:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE.  (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
016177,003453: 
016178,003454:    4453           44460        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
016179,003455:    4454           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF (LOC
016180,003456:    4455           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
016181,003457:    4456           04715        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
016182,003458:    4457           10577                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
016183,003459:    4460           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
016184,003460: 
016185,003461:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
016186,003462:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
016187,003463: 
016188,003464: 04,2577                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
016189,003465: 04,2577                                           COUNT    07/PIN                                
016190,003466: 
016191,003467: 04,2577           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
016192,003468: 04,2600           04234                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
016193,003469: 04,2601           04240                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
016194,003470: 04,2602           04410                           TC       RELDSPON                              
016195,003471: 04,2603           30001                           CA       L                                     
016196,003472: 04,2604           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
016197,003473: 04,2605           05211        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
016198,003474: 
016199,003475:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
016200,003476:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
016201,003477:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE).  IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
016202,003478:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
016203,003479:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
016204,003480: 
016205,003481:    4461                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
016206,003482:    4461                                           COUNT    02/PIN                                
016207,003483: 
016208,003484:    4461           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
016209,003485:    4462           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
016210,003486:    4463           35016                           CAF      BIT14                                 
016211,003487:    4464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016212,003488:    4465           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
016213,003489:    4466           10000                           CCS      A                                     
016214,003490:    4467           14471                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
016215,003491:    4470           14200                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
016216,003492:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
016217,003493:    4471           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2.  PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
016218,003494:    4472           14453                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
016219,003495: 
016220,003496:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
016221,003497:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
016222,003498: 
016223,003499:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
016224,003500: 
016225,003501:    4473           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
016226,003502:    4474           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
016227,003503:    4475           45016                           CS       BIT14                                 
016228,003504:    4476           00004                           INHINT                                         
016229,003505:    4477           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              
016230,003506:    4500           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
016231,003507:    4501           11043                           CCS      DSPLIST                               
016232,003508:    4502           04504                           TC       +2                                    
016233,003509:    4503           04507                           TC       RELDSP2                               #  LIST EMPTY
016234,003510:    4504           35035                           CAF      ZERO                                  
016235,003511:    4505           57043                           XCH      DSPLIST                               
016236,003512:    4506           05215                           TC       JOBWAKE                               
016237,003513:    4507           00003        RELDSP2            RELINT                                         
016238,003514:    4510           45027                           CS       BIT5                                  #  TURN OFF KEY RELEASE LIGHT
016239,003515:    4511           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11)
016240,003516:    4512           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              
016241,003517:    4513           35035                           CAF      ZERO

016361,003637: 
016362,003638:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
016363,003639:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
016364,003640:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
016365,003641: 
016366,003642:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
016367,003643:                                                                                                  #  
016368,003644:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY, RESTART.
016369,003645:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
016370,003646:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
